This is the plot of Taika Waitit's hilarious comedy that follows the adventures of the rebellious kid and his uncle. The acting is top notch and the story is simple yet engaging. It is funny and heartwarming. The wannabe 'gangsta' kid and his grumpy uncle made a hilarious pair to watch. The almost absurd and kind of slapstick humor is pleasantly complemented by the touching moments.
